const RAW_CLI_ARGS = process.argv.slice(2).map(arg => String(arg || ''));
const CLI_ARGS = new Set(RAW_CLI_ARGS.map(arg => arg.toLowerCase()));
const RUN_STARTUP_TEST = CLI_ARGS.has('--test');
const EXIT_AFTER_STARTUP_TEST = RUN_STARTUP_TEST && !CLI_ARGS.has('--test-keepalive');

function getCliArgValue(flagName) {
    const lower = String(flagName || '').toLowerCase();
    if (!lower) return '';
    for (let i = 0; i < RAW_CLI_ARGS.length; i++) {
        const arg = RAW_CLI_ARGS[i];
        const a = arg.toLowerCase();
        if (a === lower && i + 1 < RAW_CLI_ARGS.length) {
            return String(RAW_CLI_ARGS[i + 1] || '').trim();
        }
        if (a.startsWith(`${lower}=`)) {
            return String(arg.slice(flagName.length + 1) || '').trim();
        }
    }
    return '';
}

const TEST_CHANNEL_ID = (getCliArgValue('--test-channel') || process.env.DISCORD_TEST_CHANNEL_ID || '').trim();
const RAW_DUMP_MODE = RUN_STARTUP_TEST
    || CLI_ARGS.has('--raw-dump')
    || ['1', 'true', 'on'].includes((process.env.RAW_RESPONSE_DUMP || '').toLowerCase());
const RAW_DUMP_FILE = (getCliArgValue('--raw-dump-file') || process.env.RAW_RESPONSE_DUMP_FILE || '').trim();

    const FOCUS_EXP = `(async () => {
        const doc = document;
        
        // 1. Find Editor (more precise selector for the actual editable area)
        const editors = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll('div[role="textbox"] [contenteditable="plaintext-only"], div[role="textbox"] [contenteditable="true"], div[role="textbox"]:not(.xterm-helper-textarea)'));
        
        const validEditors = editors.filter(el => el.offsetParent !== null && el.offsetWidth > 0);
        const editor = validEditors.at(-1); 
        
        if (!editor) return { ok: false, error: "No editor found" };

        // 3. Focus the element so CDP Input API types into it
        editor.focus();
        
        return { ok: true, method: "focus" };

    const safeText = JSON.stringify(text);
    const EXP = `(async () => {
        const SELECTORS = ${JSON.stringify(SELECTORS)};

        function getTargetDocs() {
            const docs = [];
            const iframes = document.querySelectorAll('iframe');
            for (let i = 0; i < iframes.length; i++) {
                if ((iframes[i].src || '').includes('cascade-panel')) {
                    try {
                        if (iframes[i].contentDocument) docs.push(iframes[i].contentDocument);
                    } catch (e) {}
                }
            }
            docs.push(document);
            return docs;
        }

        function isVisible(el) {
            if (!el) return false;
            const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);
            if (style.display === 'none' || style.visibility === 'hidden' || Number(style.opacity) === 0) return false;
            if (el.offsetParent === null && style.position !== 'fixed') return false;
            const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
            return rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0;
        }

        function isSubmitButton(btn) {
            if (!btn || btn.disabled || !isVisible(btn)) return false;
            const svg = btn.querySelector('svg');
            if (svg) {
                const cls = (svg.getAttribute('class') || '') + ' ' + (btn.getAttribute('class') || '');
                if (SELECTORS.SUBMIT_BUTTON_SVG_CLASSES.some(c => cls.includes(c))) return true;
            }
            const txt = (btn.innerText || btn.getAttribute('aria-label') || '').trim().toLowerCase();
            return ['send', 'run', 'submit'].includes(txt);
        }

        function getSnapshot(doc, editor) {
            return {
                messageCount: doc.querySelectorAll('[data-message-role]').length,
                editorChars: ((editor && editor.innerText) || '').trim().length,
                cancelVisible: Boolean(doc.querySelector('[data-tooltip-id="input-send-button-cancel-tooltip"]'))
            };
        }

        function fillEditor(doc, editor, value) {
            editor.focus();
            const selection = window.getSelection();
            const range = doc.createRange();
            range.selectNodeContents(editor);
            selection.removeAllRanges();
            selection.addRange(range);

            let inserted = false;
            try {
                inserted = doc.execCommand('insertText', false, value);
            } catch (e) {}

            if (!inserted) {
                editor.textContent = value;
                try {
                    editor.dispatchEvent(new InputEvent('beforeinput', { bubbles: true, inputType: 'insertText', data: value }));
                    editor.dispatchEvent(new InputEvent('input', { bubbles: true, inputType: 'insertText', data: value }));
                } catch (e) {
                    editor.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
                }
            }
            editor.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
            editor.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
        }

        function pressEnter(editor) {
            const eventInit = { bubbles: true, cancelable: true, key: 'Enter', code: 'Enter', keyCode: 13, which: 13 };
            editor.dispatchEvent(new KeyboardEvent('keydown', eventInit));
            editor.dispatchEvent(new KeyboardEvent('keypress', eventInit));
            editor.dispatchEvent(new KeyboardEvent('keyup', eventInit));
        }

        async function trySubmit(doc, editor) {
            const before = getSnapshot(doc, editor);
            const buttons = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll('button, [role="button"]'));
            const submit = buttons.find(isSubmitButton);
            let method = 'enter';

            if (submit) {
                submit.click();
                method = 'click';
            } else {
                pressEnter(editor);
            }

            for (let i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
                await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300));
                const after = getSnapshot(doc, editor);
                const submitted =
                    after.cancelVisible ||
                    after.messageCount > before.messageCount ||
                    (before.editorChars > 0 && after.editorChars === 0);
                if (submitted) return { ok: true, method };
            }

            if (method !== 'enter') {
                pressEnter(editor);
                for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
                    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300));
                    const after = getSnapshot(doc, editor);
                    const submitted =
                        after.cancelVisible ||
                        after.messageCount > before.messageCount ||
                        (before.editorChars > 0 && after.editorChars === 0);
                    if (submitted) return { ok: true, method: 'enter' };
                }
            }

            return { ok: false, error: 'submit_not_confirmed' };
        }

        const docs = getTargetDocs();
        for (const doc of docs) {
            const editors = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll(SELECTORS.CHAT_INPUT)).filter(isVisible);
            const editor = editors.at(-1);
            if (!editor) continue;

            fillEditor(doc, editor, ${safeText});
            await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 400));
            const result = await trySubmit(doc, editor);
            if (result.ok) return result;
        }

        return { ok: false, error: 'No editor or submission not confirmed in this context' };

            // STEP 1: Focus the input field
            const focusRes = await cdp.call("Runtime.evaluate", { expression: FOCUS_EXP, returnByValue: true, awaitPromise: true, contextId: ctx.id });

            if (focusRes.result?.value?.ok) {
                // STEP 2: Use Native CDP Input API to bulk type text (Safer for CJK processing)
                await cdp.call("Input.insertText", { text: text });

                // To reliably trigger React's input event handler and enable the submit button, 
                // we send a space and delete it immediately.
                await cdp.call("Input.dispatchKeyEvent", { type: 'char', text: ' ' });
                await cdp.call("Input.dispatchKeyEvent", { type: 'keyDown', key: 'Backspace', code: 'Backspace', text: '\\b' });
                await cdp.call("Input.dispatchKeyEvent", { type: 'keyUp', key: 'Backspace', code: 'Backspace' });

                // Wait briefly for React/Monaco state to update and button to appear
                await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300));

                // STEP 3: Press Enter key via CDP
                await cdp.call("Input.dispatchKeyEvent", { type: 'keyDown', key: 'Enter', code: 'Enter', text: '\\r' });
                await cdp.call("Input.dispatchKeyEvent", { type: 'keyUp', key: 'Enter', code: 'Enter' });

                logInteraction('INJECT', `Sent: (Censored length: ${text.length}) (Context: ${ctx.id})`);
                return { ok: true };
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(`[Injection Error] Context ${ctx.id}: ${e.message}`);

        function findAgentFrame(win) {
             const iframes = document.querySelectorAll('iframe');
             for(let i=0; i<iframes.length; i++) {
                 if(iframes[i].src.includes('cascade-panel')) {
                     try { return iframes[i].contentDocument; } catch(e){}
                 }
             }
             return document;

<<<<<<< ours
        for (const doc of docs) {
            // UI下部の入力ボックス内にあるボタン全体を調べる
            const cancelBtn = doc.querySelector('[data-tooltip-id="input-send-button-cancel-tooltip"]');
            const sendBtn   = doc.querySelector('[data-tooltip-id="input-send-button-tooltip"]') || doc.querySelector('[data-tooltip-id="input-send-button-pending-tooltip"]');
            
            // Antigravityの最新UIでは、CancelボタンもSendボタンも常にDOM上に存在し offsetParent も null にならない。
            // 実際に表示が切り替わる際は、内部の svg アイコンがDOMに追加/削除されることで表現されている。
            if (cancelBtn && sendBtn) {
                 const cancelSvg = cancelBtn.querySelector('svg');
                 if (cancelSvg) {
                     return true;
                 }
                 // SVGがない場合はCancelボタンは機能していない（＝生成中ではない）
                 return false;
            }
             
            // または「Stop」というラベルがある旧形式のボタンを探す
            const buttons = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll('button'));
            for (const btn of buttons) {
                const txt = (btn.innerText || '').trim().toLowerCase();
                if ((txt === 'stop' || txt === '停止') && btn.offsetParent !== null) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }

        const uiNoiseKeywords = [
            'Progress Updates', 'Background Steps', 'Running command', 'Task less than',
            'Files Edited', 'Injecting message', '[INJECT]', 'Agent can plan before',
            'Ask anything, @ to mention', 'Review Changes', 'AI Shortcuts'

        const candidates = [];
        let order = 0;

        function cleanText(text) {
            const lines = String(text || '')
                .split('\\n')
                .map(l => l.trim())
                .filter(Boolean);
            const filtered = lines.filter(l =>
                !l.startsWith('Injecting message') &&
                !l.startsWith('[INJECT]') &&
                !l.includes('Context: ') &&
                !l.startsWith('Ran command ')
            );
            return filtered.join('\\n').trim();
        }

        function collectCandidate(node, roleScore) {
            if (!node || node.offsetParent === null) return;
            if (node.closest && node.closest('.antigravity-agent-side-panel')) return;

            const target = node.querySelector?.('.leading-relaxed.select-text, .prose, .markdown-body') || node;
            const text = cleanText(target.innerText || '');
            if (text.length < 8) return;

            let score = roleScore;
            const lower = text.toLowerCase();
            for (const kw of uiNoiseKeywords) {
                if (lower.includes(kw.toLowerCase())) score -= 80;
            }
            score += Math.min(40, Math.floor(text.length / 40));
            score += Math.min(20, Math.floor(order / 10));

            candidates.push({
                text,
                score,
                order,
                images: Array.from(target.querySelectorAll('img')).map(img => img.src).filter(Boolean)
            });
        }

        for (const doc of docs) {
            const assistantNodes = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll('[data-message-role="assistant"]'));
            assistantNodes.forEach((el) => {
                order += 1;
                collectCandidate(el, 120);
            });

            const botMessageBlocks = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll('.text-ide-message-block-bot-color, .chat-message.assistant'));
            botMessageBlocks.forEach((el) => {
                order += 1;
                collectCandidate(el, 80);
            });
        }

        if (candidates.length === 0) return null;
        candidates.sort((a, b) => (b.score - a.score) || (b.order - a.order));
        const best = candidates[0];
        return { text: best.text, images: best.images, score: best.score };
    })()`;

    let best = null;
    for (const ctx of cdp.contexts) {

function getTextHash(text) {
    let h = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) h = ((h << 5) - h + text.charCodeAt(i)) | 0;
    return String(h >>> 0);
}

function isLowQualityResponse(text) {
    const t = (text || '').trim();
    if (t.length === 0) return true;
    if (t.length <= 2) return true;
    if (/^([a-zA-Zぁ-んァ-ヶ一-龠])\1{2,}$/.test(t)) return true;
    if (/^[sS]+$/.test(t)) return true;
    const badStarts = ['Injecting message', '[INJECT]', 'Running command', 'Background Steps', 'Progress Updates'];
    if (badStarts.some(prefix => t.startsWith(prefix))) return true;
    return false;

            function getTargetDocs() {
                const docs = [];
                const iframes = document.querySelectorAll('iframe');
                for (let i = 0; i < iframes.length; i++) {
                    if (!String(iframes[i].src || '').includes('cascade-panel')) continue;
                    try {
                        const d = iframes[i].contentDocument;
                        if (d) docs.push(d);
                    } catch (e) {}
                }
                if (docs.length === 0) docs.push(document);
                return docs;
            }

            function isVisible(el) {
                if (!el) return false;
                const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);
                if (style.display === 'none' || style.visibility === 'hidden' || Number(style.opacity) === 0) return false;
                const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
                return rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0;
            }

            function normalizeText(text) {
                return String(text || '').replace(/\\r/g, '').replace(/[ \\t]+$/gm, '').trim();
            }

            function clipText(text, maxLen) {
                const s = String(text || '');
                const n = Number(maxLen || 12000);
                if (s.length <= n) return s;
                return s.slice(0, n) + "\\n...[truncated " + (s.length - n) + " chars]";
            }

            function normalizeLine(line) {
                return String(line || '').trim().toLowerCase();
            }

            function isUiChromeLine(line) {
                const t = normalizeLine(line);
                if (!t) return true;
                if (/^[+-]\\d+$/.test(t)) return true;
                if (/^\\d+\\s+chars[驕ｯ・ｶ繝ｻ・｢繝ｻ繧托ｽｽ・ｷ].*$/i.test(t)) return true;
                if (t === 'analyzed' || t.startsWith('analyzed ')) return true;
                if (t === 'thinking' || t === 'generating' || t === 'generating..' || t === 'generating...') return true;
                if (t.startsWith('thought for ')) return true;
                if (t === 'planning' || t === 'fast') return true;
                if (t === 'review changes') return true;
                if (t === 'add context' || t === 'media' || t === 'mentions' || t === 'workflows') return true;
                if (t === 'conversation mode' || t === 'model' || t === 'new' || t === 'send') return true;
                if (/^\\d+\\s+files?\\s+with\\s+changes$/i.test(t)) return true;
                if (t === 'git graph') return true;
                if (t === 'antigravity - settings') return true;
                if (t === 'agq') return true;
                if (/^pro\\s+\\d+%\\s+flash\\s+\\d+%/i.test(t)) return true;
                if (/^(css|html|javascript|typescript|json)$/i.test(t)) return true;
                if (/^(crlf|lf|utf-8|utf8)$/i.test(t)) return true;
                if (/^ln\\s+\\d+,\\s*col\\s+\\d+$/i.test(t)) return true;
                if (t === 'reject all' || t === 'accept all') return true;
                if (t.includes('ask anything, @ to mention')) return true;
                if (t.startsWith('agent can plan before executing tasks')) return true;
                if (t.startsWith('agent will execute tasks directly')) return true;
                if (t.startsWith('prioritizing specific tools')) return true;
                if (t.startsWith('gemini ') || t.startsWith('claude ') || t.startsWith('gpt-')) return true;
                return false;
            }

            function getMeaningfulLines(text) {
                return String(text || '')
                    .replace(/\\r/g, '')
                    .split('\\n')
                    .map(l => l.trim())
                    .filter(Boolean)
                    .filter(l => !isUiChromeLine(l));
            }

            function scoreMeaningfulText(text) {
                const lines = getMeaningfulLines(text);
                if (lines.length === 0) return { score: 0, text: '' };
                let score = 0;
                for (const l of lines) score += Math.min(l.length, 120);
                return { score, text: lines.join('\\n') };
            }

            function normalizeMarkdown(text) {
                return String(text || '')
                    .replace(/\\r/g, '')
                    .replace(/[ \\t]+\\n/g, '\\n')
                    .replace(/\\n{3,}/g, '\\n\\n')
                    .trim();
            }

            function hasChangeSummary(text) {
                const t = String(text || '');
                if (!t) return false;
                return (
                    /(^|\\n)\\s*Edited(?:\\s+[+-]\\d+\\s+[+-]\\d+)?\\s*($|\\n)/i.test(t) ||
                    /(^|\\n)\\s*[+-]\\d+\\s*($|\\n)/m.test(t) ||
                    /\\b\\d+\\s+insertions?\\s*\\(\\+\\)/i.test(t) ||
                    /\\b\\d+\\s+deletions?\\s*\\(-\\)/i.test(t)
                );
            }

            function extractChangeLines(text) {
                const lines = String(text || '')
                    .split('\\n')
                    .map(l => l.trim())
                    .filter(Boolean);
                const out = [];
                const seen = new Set();

                function pushLine(line) {
                    const key = line.toLowerCase();
                    if (seen.has(key)) return;
                    seen.add(key);
                    out.push(line);
                }

                for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
                    const line = lines[i];
                    if (
                        /^edited(?:\\s+[+-]\\d+\\s+[+-]\\d+)?$/i.test(line) ||
                        /^[+-]\\d+$/.test(line) ||
                        /^\\d+\\s+insertions?\\s*\\(\\+\\)\\s*$/i.test(line) ||
                        /^\\d+\\s+deletions?\\s*\\(-\\)\\s*$/i.test(line) ||
                        /^\\d+\\s+insertions?\\s*\\(\\+\\)\\s+\\d+\\s+deletions?\\s*\\(-\\)\\s*$/i.test(line)
                    ) {
                        pushLine(line);
                    }
                }
                return out;
            }

            function collectMessageNodes(doc) {
                const selectors = [
                    '[data-message-role]',
                    '[data-testid*="assistant"]',
                    '[data-testid*="message"]',
                    'article',
                    '[role="article"]'
                ];
                const nodes = [];
                const seen = new Set();
                for (const selector of selectors) {
                    const list = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll(selector));
                    for (const node of list) {
                        if (!node || seen.has(node) || !isVisible(node)) continue;
                        seen.add(node);
                        nodes.push(node);
                    }
                }

                nodes.sort((a, b) => {
                    if (a === b) return 0;
                    const pos = a.compareDocumentPosition(b);
                    if (pos & Node.DOCUMENT_POSITION_FOLLOWING) return -1;
                    if (pos & Node.DOCUMENT_POSITION_PRECEDING) return 1;
                    return 0;
                });
                return nodes;
            }

            function collectMessageTailText(doc) {
                const nodes = collectMessageNodes(doc);
                const texts = [];
                const textSeen = new Set();
                for (const node of nodes) {
                    if (node.querySelectorAll && node.querySelectorAll('[data-message-role]').length > 5) continue;
                    const text = normalizeText(node.innerText || node.textContent);
                    if (!text || text.length > 10000) continue;
                    const meaningful = scoreMeaningfulText(text).text || text;
                    const key = meaningful.toLowerCase();
                    if (textSeen.has(key)) continue;
                    textSeen.add(key);
                    texts.push(meaningful);
                }
                if (texts.length === 0) return '';
                return texts.slice(-6).join('\\n\\n').trim();
            }

            function getMarkdownRoot(node) {
                if (!node || !node.querySelectorAll) return node;

                const candidates = [];
                try {
                    if (typeof node.matches === 'function' && node.matches('.markdown-body, .prose, [class*="markdown"], [data-testid*="markdown"]')) {
                        candidates.push(node);
                    }
                } catch (e) {}

                const query = '.markdown-body, .prose, [class*="markdown"], [data-testid*="markdown"]';
                for (const el of Array.from(node.querySelectorAll(query))) {
                    if (el && isVisible(el)) candidates.push(el);
                }
                if (candidates.length === 0) return node;

                candidates.sort((a, b) => {
                    const la = String(a.innerText || '').length;
                    const lb = String(b.innerText || '').length;
                    return lb - la;
                });
                return candidates[0] || node;
            }

            function inlineContent(node) {
                if (!node) return '';
                if (node.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE) {
                    return String(node.nodeValue || '').replace(/\\s+/g, ' ');
                }
                if (node.nodeType !== Node.ELEMENT_NODE) return '';

                const tag = String(node.tagName || '').toLowerCase();
                if (tag === 'br') return '\\n';
                if (tag === 'button' || tag === 'input' || tag === 'textarea' || tag === 'select' || tag === 'svg' || tag === 'path') return '';
                if (tag === 'code' && !(node.parentElement && String(node.parentElement.tagName || '').toLowerCase() === 'pre')) {
                    const code = String(node.textContent || '').trim();
                    if (!code) return '';
                    const backtick = String.fromCharCode(96);
                    return backtick + code + backtick;
                }

                let inner = '';
                for (const child of Array.from(node.childNodes || [])) {
                    inner += inlineContent(child);
                }
                inner = inner
                    .replace(/[ \\t]+\\n/g, '\\n')
                    .replace(/\\n[ \\t]+/g, '\\n')
                    .replace(/[ \\t]{2,}/g, ' ');

                if (tag === 'strong' || tag === 'b') {
                    const t = inner.trim();
                    return t ? ('**' + t + '**') : '';
                }
                if (tag === 'em' || tag === 'i') {
                    const t = inner.trim();
                    return t ? ('*' + t + '*') : '';
                }
                if (tag === 'a') {
                    const href = String(node.getAttribute('href') || '').trim();
                    const label = String(inner || href).trim();
                    if (!label) return '';
                    return href ? ('[' + label + '](' + href + ')') : label;
                }
                if (tag === 'img') {
                    const src = String(node.getAttribute('src') || '').trim();
                    const alt = String(node.getAttribute('alt') || '').trim();
                    if (!src && !alt) return '';
                    return '![' + alt + '](' + src + ')';
                }
                return inner;
            }

            function renderList(node, ordered) {
                const items = Array.from(node.children || []).filter(el => String(el.tagName || '').toLowerCase() === 'li');
                if (items.length === 0) return '';

                const lines = [];
                for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                    const li = items[i];
                    const body = (renderNode(li) || inlineContent(li) || '').trim();
                    if (!body) continue;

                    const rawLines = body
                        .split('\\n')
                        .map(line => line.replace(/\\s+$/g, ''))
                        .filter((line, idx, arr) => !(idx === arr.length - 1 && !line));
                    if (rawLines.length === 0) continue;

                    const prefix = ordered ? (String(i + 1) + '. ') : '- ';
                    lines.push(prefix + rawLines[0]);
                    for (let j = 1; j < rawLines.length; j++) {
                        lines.push('   ' + rawLines[j]);
                    }
                }
                return lines.length > 0 ? (lines.join('\\n') + '\\n\\n') : '';
            }

            function renderNode(node) {
                if (!node) return '';
                if (node.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE) return inlineContent(node);
                if (node.nodeType !== Node.ELEMENT_NODE) return '';

                const tag = String(node.tagName || '').toLowerCase();
                if (tag === 'script' || tag === 'style' || tag === 'noscript') return '';

                if (tag === 'h1' || tag === 'h2' || tag === 'h3' || tag === 'h4' || tag === 'h5' || tag === 'h6') {
                    const level = Number(tag.slice(1)) || 1;
                    const title = inlineContent(node).trim();
                    if (!title) return '';
                    return '#'.repeat(Math.max(1, Math.min(6, level))) + ' ' + title + '\\n\\n';
                }
                if (tag === 'p') {
                    const body = inlineContent(node).trim();
                    return body ? (body + '\\n\\n') : '';
                }
                if (tag === 'pre') {
                    const code = String(node.innerText || node.textContent || '').replace(/\\r/g, '').replace(/\\n+$/g, '');
                    if (!code) return '';
                    const backtick = String.fromCharCode(96);
                    const fence = backtick + backtick + backtick;
                    return fence + '\\n' + code + '\\n' + fence + '\\n\\n';
                }
                if (tag === 'ul') return renderList(node, false);
                if (tag === 'ol') return renderList(node, true);
                if (tag === 'li') {
                    let combined = '';
                    for (const child of Array.from(node.childNodes || [])) {
                        combined += renderNode(child);
                    }
                    if (!combined.trim()) combined = inlineContent(node);
                    return normalizeMarkdown(combined);
                }
                if (tag === 'blockquote') {
                    const body = normalizeMarkdown(Array.from(node.childNodes || []).map(renderNode).join('') || inlineContent(node));
                    if (!body) return '';
                    const quoted = body.split('\\n').map(line => '> ' + line).join('\\n');
                    return quoted + '\\n\\n';
                }
                if (tag === 'hr') return '---\\n\\n';
                if (tag === 'table') {
                    const t = normalizeText(node.innerText || node.textContent);
                    return t ? (t + '\\n\\n') : '';
                }

                const blockTags = new Set(['div', 'section', 'article', 'main']);
                const children = Array.from(node.childNodes || []);
                let rendered = '';
                for (const child of children) {
                    rendered += renderNode(child);
                }

                if (blockTags.has(tag)) {
                    const text = normalizeMarkdown(rendered);
                    if (text) return text + '\\n\\n';
                    const inline = inlineContent(node).trim();
                    return inline ? (inline + '\\n\\n') : '';
                }
                return rendered || inlineContent(node);
            }

            function renderMarkdown(node) {
                const root = getMarkdownRoot(node);
                return normalizeMarkdown(renderNode(root));
            }

            function collectMessageTailMarkdown(doc) {
                const nodes = collectMessageNodes(doc);
                const markdowns = [];
                const seen = new Set();
                for (const node of nodes) {
                    if (node.querySelectorAll && node.querySelectorAll('[data-message-role]').length > 5) continue;
                    const md = renderMarkdown(node);
                    if (!md || md.length > 20000) continue;
                    const key = md.toLowerCase();
                    if (seen.has(key)) continue;
                    seen.add(key);
                    markdowns.push(md);
                }
                if (markdowns.length === 0) return '';
                return markdowns.slice(-1)[0] || '';
            }

            function pickFromDoc(doc) {
                const selectorGroups = [
                    ['[data-message-role="assistant"]', 140],
                    ['[data-testid*="assistant"]', 130],
                    ['article [data-message-role]', 120],
                    ['[data-message-role]', 110],
                    ['.markdown-body', 100],
                    ['.prose', 95],
                    ['[class*="assistant"]', 90],
                    ['article', 80],
                    ['[role="article"]', 75],
                    ['[class*="message"]', 70]
                ];

                const seen = new Set();
                let best = null;
                let order = 0;

                for (const [selector, baseScore] of selectorGroups) {
                    const nodes = Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll(selector));
                    for (const node of nodes) {
                        if (!node || seen.has(node)) continue;
                        seen.add(node);
                        order += 1;
                        if (!isVisible(node)) continue;

                        if (baseScore <= 80 && node.querySelectorAll && node.querySelectorAll('[data-message-role]').length > 6) {
                            continue;
                        }

                        const text = normalizeText(node.innerText || node.textContent);
                        if (!text) continue;
                        const meaningfulInfo = scoreMeaningfulText(text);

                        const role = String(node.getAttribute('data-message-role') || '').toLowerCase();
                        const klass = String(node.className || '').toLowerCase();
                        const assistantScore = (role === 'assistant' ? 60 : 0) + (klass.includes('assistant') ? 25 : 0);
                        const changeScore = hasChangeSummary(text) ? 4000 : 0;
                        const textPenalty = Math.max(0, Math.min(text.length - meaningfulInfo.text.length, 4000));
                        const score =
                            baseScore +
                            assistantScore +
                            changeScore +
                            Math.min(meaningfulInfo.score, 5000) +
                            Math.min(text.length, 1200) -
                            Math.floor(textPenalty * 0.2) +
                            order;

                        if (!best || score >= best.score) {
                            best = { node, text: meaningfulInfo.text || text, rawText: text, score, selector };
                        }
                    }
                }

                const bodyText = normalizeText((doc.body && doc.body.innerText) || '');
                const changeLines = extractChangeLines(bodyText);
                const tailText = collectMessageTailText(doc);
                const tailMarkdown = collectMessageTailMarkdown(doc);

                let finalText = best ? (best.text || best.rawText) : '';
                let finalSelector = best ? best.selector : 'none';
                let finalMarkdown = best && best.node ? renderMarkdown(best.node) : '';

                if (tailText) {
                    const tailHasChanges = hasChangeSummary(tailText);
                    const bestHasChanges = hasChangeSummary(finalText);
                    if ((tailHasChanges && !bestHasChanges) || (tailText.length > finalText.length && finalText.length < 500)) {
                        finalText = tailText;
                        if (tailMarkdown) finalMarkdown = tailMarkdown;
                        finalSelector = 'message-tail';
                    }
                }

                if (!finalText && bodyText) {
                    finalText = bodyText;
                    const bodyMarkdown = renderMarkdown(doc.body);
                    if (bodyMarkdown) finalMarkdown = bodyMarkdown;
                    finalSelector = 'body-fallback';
                }
                if (!finalText) return null;

                const meaningfulFinal = scoreMeaningfulText(finalText);
                if (meaningfulFinal.score < 40) {
                    const bodyMeaningfulLines = getMeaningfulLines(bodyText);
                    if (bodyMeaningfulLines.length > 0) {
                        finalText = bodyMeaningfulLines.slice(-120).join('\\n');
                        finalMarkdown = finalText;
                        finalSelector = 'body-meaningful-fallback';
                    }
                }

                if (changeLines.length > 0) {
                    const lower = finalText.toLowerCase();
                    const missing = changeLines.filter(line => !lower.includes(line.toLowerCase()));
                    if (missing.length > 0) {
                        finalText = (missing.join('\\n') + '\\n\\n' + finalText).trim();
                        const missingMd = missing.join('\\n');
                        finalMarkdown = (missingMd + '\\n\\n' + (finalMarkdown || finalText)).trim();
                    }
                }

                if (!finalMarkdown) finalMarkdown = finalText;

                let domDebug = null;
                if (best && best.node) {
                    let node = best.node;
                    let selectedSelector = best.selector || '';
                    const nodeTextLower = normalizeText(node.innerText || node.textContent || '').toLowerCase();
                    const uiChromeSignals = [
                        'ask anything, @ to mention, / for workflows',
                        'conversation mode',
                        'agent can plan before executing tasks',
                        'add context',
                        'review changes'
                    ];
                    const looksLikeUiPanel = uiChromeSignals.some(signal => nodeTextLower.includes(signal));
                    if (looksLikeUiPanel && doc.body) {
                        node = doc.body;
                        selectedSelector = 'body-domdebug-fallback';
                    }
                    const root = getMarkdownRoot(node);
                    domDebug = {
                        selectedSelector,
                        nodeTag: String(node.tagName || '').toLowerCase(),
                        nodeClass: String(node.className || ''),
                        nodeRole: String(node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-message-role') || ''),
                        nodeText: clipText(node.innerText || node.textContent || '', 8000),
                        nodeInnerHTML: String(node.innerHTML || ''),
                        nodeOuterHTML: String(node.outerHTML || ''),
                        markdownRootTag: root ? String(root.tagName || '').toLowerCase() : '',
                        markdownRootClass: root ? String(root.className || '') : '',
                        markdownRootOuterHTML: root ? String(root.outerHTML || '') : '',
                        bodyTailText: clipText(bodyText.slice(-4000), 4000)
                    };
                }

                return {
                    text: finalText,
                    markdown: finalMarkdown,
                    images: best && best.node ? Array.from(best.node.querySelectorAll('img')).map(img => img.src).filter(Boolean) : [],
                    score: (best ? best.score : 0) + (hasChangeSummary(finalText) ? 5000 : 0) + (changeLines.length * 300) + Math.min(finalMarkdown.length, 1200),
                    selector: finalSelector,
                    changeLinesCount: changeLines.length,
                    messageRoleCount: doc.querySelectorAll('[data-message-role]').length,
                    domDebug
                };
            }

            const docs = getTargetDocs();
            let picked = null;
            for (const d of docs) {
                const current = pickFromDoc(d);
                if (!current) continue;
                if (!picked || current.score > picked.score || (current.score === picked.score && current.text.length > picked.text.length)) {
                    picked = current;
                }
            }
            return picked;
        })()`;
    let best = null;
    for (const ctx of cdp.contexts) {
        try {
            const evalPromise = cdp.call("Runtime.evaluate", { expression: EXP, returnByValue: true, contextId: ctx.id });
            const timeoutPromise = new Promise((_, reject) => setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('getLastResponse timeout')), 10000));
            const res = await Promise.race([evalPromise, timeoutPromise]);
            const value = res.result?.value;
            const text = String(value?.text || '').trim();
            if (!text) continue;
            const markdown = String(value?.markdown || '').trim();
            const score = Number(value?.score || 0);
            if (!best || score > best.score || (score === best.score && text.length > best.text.length)) {
                best = {
                    text,
                    markdown: markdown || text,
                    images: Array.isArray(value?.images) ? value.images : [],
                    score,
                    selector: value?.selector || 'unknown',
                    messageRoleCount: Number(value?.messageRoleCount || 0),
                    domDebug: (value?.domDebug && typeof value.domDebug === 'object') ? value.domDebug : null,
                    contextId: ctx.id
                };
            }
        } catch (e) {
            logInteraction('ERROR', `getLastResponse context ${ctx.id} failed: ${e?.message || String(e)}`);
        }
    }
    return best;

    queueByChannel(message, async () => {
        const trimmed = messageText.trim();
        const agMatch = trimmed.match(/^!ag\s+([\s\S]+)/i);
        if (agMatch) {
            const taskText = agMatch[1].trim();
            if (!taskText) {
                await message.reply('⚠️ 使い方: `!ag <依頼内容>`');
                return;
            }
            const cdp = await ensureCDP();
            if (!cdp) {
                await message.reply("❌ CDP not found. Is Antigravity running?");
                return;
            }
            await message.react('🛠️');
            await handleAntigravityDelegation(message, taskText, cdp);
            return;
        }

        await message.react('💬');
        await handleCodexChat(message, messageText);
    }).catch(async (e) => {
        console.error('[MESSAGE_HANDLER_ERROR]', e);
        try { await message.reply(`⚠️ 処理中にエラーが発生しました: ${e.message}`); } catch { }
    });
